   function onDidomiInteraction(action) {
return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
const formData = new FormData();
const httpRequest = new XMLHttpRequest();
const url = '/gs_cb/index.cfm?event=tracking:ajax.cmpAction';
formData.append('action', action);
httpRequest.open('POST', url, true);
httpRequest.onload = function () {
if (this.status >= 200 && this.status < 300) {
resolve(httpRequest.response);
} else {
reject({
status: this.status,
statusText: httpRequest.statusText
});
}
};
httpRequest.onerror = function () {
reject({
status: this.status,
statusText: httpRequest.statusText
});
};
httpRequest.send(formData);
});
}
window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', e => {
const observerBody = new MutationObserver(mutations => {

.filter(node => node.id === 'didomi-host')
.forEach(node => {
observerDidomiHost.observe(node, { subtree: true, childList: true });
observerBody.disconnect();
});
});
});
const observerDidomiHost = new MutationObserver(mutations => {
mutations.forEach(mutation => {
Array.from(mutation.addedNodes)
.forEach(node => {
if (node.id === 'didomi-popup') {
onDidomiInteraction('didomi-consent-popup-view');
observerDidomiHost.disconnect();
}
});
});
});

}, {once: true});
document.addEventListener('mouseup', e => {
e = e || window.event;
const eTarget = e.target || e.srcElement;
if (eTarget.id === 'didomi-notice-learn-more-button') {
onDidomiInteraction('didomi-notice-learn-more-button-click');
} else if (eTarget.id === 'didomi-notice-agree-button') {
onDidomiInteraction('didomi-notice-agree-button-click');
} else if (eTarget.closest('.didomi-consent-popup-preferences')) {
const clickedButton = eTarget.classList.contains('didomi-button') ? eTarget : eTarget.closest('.didomi-button');
if (!clickedButton) {
return;
}
if (clickedButton.classList.contains('didomi-button-standard')) {
onDidomiInteraction('didomi-consent-popup-preferences-deny-all-click');
} else if (clickedButton.classList.contains('didomi-button-highlight')) {
onDidomiInteraction(clickedButton.textContent === 'Speichern' ?
'didomi-consent-popup-preferences-individual-selection-save-click' :
'didomi-consent-popup-preferences-accept-all-click'
);
}
} else if (eTarget.classList.contains('didomi-notice-view-partners-link-click')) {
onDidomiInteraction('didomi-notice-view-partners-link-click');
} else if (eTarget.parentElement && eTarget.parentElement.classList.contains('didomi-notice-view-partners-link')) {
onDidomiInteraction('didomi-notice-view-partners-link-click');
}
});

      <section class="grid grid-12 no-grid-gap">
       <div>
        <section class="grid grid-12 highlight sm-hide-category noLink" id="section105" style="order:2;">

  <script>
   window.didomiOnReady = window.didomiOnReady || [];
window.didomiOnReady.push(function (Didomi) {
if (Didomi.isUserConsentStatusPartial() || Didomi.shouldConsentBeCollected()) {
$('#content').addClass('modal-cmp');
$('#cmp-modal').modal({
backdrop: 'static'
});
onDidomiInteraction('didomi-consent-popup-view');
}
});
function acceptCmp() {
Didomi.setUserAgreeToAll(true);
onDidomiInteraction('didomi-accept-all-click');
$('#cmp-modal').hide();
$('body').removeClass('modal-open');
$('.modal-backdrop').remove();
$('#content').removeClass('modal-cmp');
}
$('.cmp-accept').on('click', function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
acceptCmp();
});
$('.cmp-show-preferences').on('click', function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
Didomi.preferences.show();
onDidomiInteraction('didomi-preferences-view');
});
$('.cmp-show-vendors').on('click', function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
Didomi.preferences.show('vendors');
onDidomiInteraction('didomi-preferences-view');
});
$('#cmp-content a:not(.no-link)').on('click', function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
onDidomiInteraction('didomi-' + $(e.target).data('interactionId') + '-click').then(() => {
window.location = e.target.href;
});
});
  </script>
